2b2(mdo): byal sangs rgyas kyis shin zhab cing / dam pa'i chos kyi yi ge bcu gnyis bshad pa yi ge'i 'bru ni mangs/ gzung ni rgya ches pas khong du chud cing 'tshal bar bgyi ba'ang dka'/ 
2b3(mdo): chos 'di kun blta zhing rjes kyang mi chod na/ sangs rgyas kyis byams shing thugs rjes gzigs te/ theg pa chen po'i chos yang dag pa'i bden pa bye brag phyed par bshad de/ sems can/ 
2b4(mdo): rnams yang dgra pa'i sman bsnang po thob par bgyis te// nad gdug go cog spos pAr bstir smon to// sangs rgyas kyis byang chub sems dpa' nam mkhe'i mdzod la bka' stsal pa/ shin/ 
2b5(mdo): du dge'o// shin du dge'o// rigs kyi bu po khyod kyis sems can rnams kyi phyir 'di lta bu'i don chen po 'dri nus pa bsod nams chen po thob ste/ bsam gyis mi khyab po// ngas khyod la
2b6(mdo): yang dag pa'i bden pa/ thegs pa chen po'i chos bye brag byed pa/ mi 'gyur ba'i gzhung rdzogs pa bshad do// ci'i phyir zhes byas na/ sems can rnams mya ngan dang bral bar bya ba'i phyir
2b7(mdo): sems can dmyal ba'i nyon mongs pa las phyin cing yul gtsang mar skye bar bya ba'i phyir ro// yang dag par grol thar cing skye shi la sna 'das par bya ba'i phyir khyed rnams kun sems gcig
2b8(mdo): tu soms shig dang khyed la go bar bshad do// de nas pa la mang po kun shin tu dga' gzha' ste/ 'badad kyis kyang tshig 'thun par tshig car sbas pa

3b2(mdo): sangs rgyastsa la ga sol pa/ bcom ldan 'das yang dag par gshegs pas meg pa chen po'i chos yang dag pa'i gzugs shin du 'a ci gces bya/ bla rnam mchis pa'i sran 'azang po dang
3b3(mdo): theg pa gcig gi bden pa'i nang du 'dug pa bshad na/ slan chad kyi sems can mi gtsang ba'i las gsum gyi sa dran pa bcu'i lus bstis te/ log sred kyi las spyad pas rmya ba dang gzhi phra'ing
3b4(mdo): zhan te/ sems la gzungs su gzung ba'ang dka' nas sman dang nad kyang gal te mi mthun na thabs ji ltar bgyis na theg pa chen po'i nang du 'jug par rung / sangs rgyas kyis byang chub sem
3b5(mdo): dpa' nam mkha' mdzod la bka' stsal pa/ ngal thabs yod kyis theg pa chen po la 'jug par bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' nam mkha' mdzod kyis sangs rgyas la gsol pa/ bcom
3b6(mdo): rnams bdag gis lan tsun thos pa yang dag par gshegs pa ste rtseg pa chen po'i ma ni ldan pa drug gi chos bshad/ meg pa par ma'i ye rgyu rkyen bcug nyis
3b7(mdo): bshad/ theg pa chung ngu'i mi lnga ni bden pa bzhi'i chos bshad/ log sred kyi ma la ni dge ba bcu'i chos bshad de/ kun kyang nad kyi gzugs dang sbyar nas chos kyi sman bzang po bshad

5a3(mdo): no nog sems kyi yan lag g.yos pas rang bzhin gyi stobs gnyis smod do// gnyis shes bya ba gang yin zhes byas na/ gcig ni 'dum ched kyi phyir gapos te sems kyi yan+da lag
5a4(mdo): bzhin gyi stobs so// gnyis ni 'du mched kyi phyir ma lags kyi bdag gi sems la rang langs te de ni bdag gi rang bzhin gyi stobs so// rigs kyi bu po de sems can rnams kyi rang bzhi

5a6(mdo): khyod la sogs pa byang chub sems dpas sems can zhig bstan cing drang na yang sems 'dug par ston cig/ byang chub sems dpa' nam mkha' mdzod kyis sangs

344a3(mdo): rol du phyin pa bstan par zungs shig/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi thabs mkhas pa'i gsang ba'i le'ur zungs shig ces/ bcom ldan 'das dgyes shing / de skad ces bka' stsal ba dang / 
344a4(mdo): / dga' bo dang / byang chub sems dnga' sems dpa' chen po ye shes pa dang / lha dang me da la ma yin dang / dri bangar bcas pa'i 'jig rten rnams bcom ldan 'das
344a5(mdo): bka' bral pa la mngon par dga'o// tha'as mkhas pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdordzogs so//  khrag sug brgyas lam po gnas
